< Review>
This is such a cute little bookstore. Great for book-lovers who just want to roam the shelves and find interesting reads! I love that they have a separate upper floor for poetry, and that they encourage you to stop and sit and read a book. They also have a lot of spotlighted books and staff recommendations that I feel like I can actually take seriously. If only I had more time to explore when I was here!</Review>

< Text>
I needed some graph paper (the kind engineers use a good deal of, or used to at any rate) so I called to ask if they had a stationery section. The young lady who answered obviously didn't know the meaning of the word. "Is that a book?" I mean, stationary versus stationery. I learned that in 5th grade elementary school. "Stationery?" "No, I move all around!" 5th grade humor of 60 years ago. Or our teacher at least thought it was funny. Along with "Empty barrels make the most noise." Another line I didn't appreciate until I got much older. I think of it every time some loudmouth makes an absolute fool of him/her self. Dollar Store, known for serving primarily poorer people, even has a sign posting their "Stationery" section (alas with no paper with ruling to help me draw graphs, hence the reason for my call to CSULB). Maybe I will try 99 cents Store. CSULB Bookstore staff doesn't even understand the concept of paper or notebooks anymore--- from what I gather.  Do they just text everything? Even x-y data plots?   Does the latest Apple iphone do that now? No idea, but I doubt it. I also wonder whether CSULB engineering students ever plot anything anymore. Or do they just leave that to their calculators? In that case, how do they "turn in" their results for grading? is everything now just a b c d e "multiple guess" perhaps? Where even a monkey can score 20%?
I know the stuff I am talking about is still manufactured (even if slide rules aren't). They sell it on Amazon. The same light green colored stuff I used to buy 50 years ago. Even if CSULB doesn't. This place really deserves an 8 star rating. Service was out of this world. The food was amazing. We ordered a thin crust pizza, the crust was thinner than a saltine cracker but oh my gosh. It packed so much flavor without it being all bread. The thin crust was not overly crunchy, just simply perfect. The alcoholic cocktails are made with 3 OZ. of alcohol instead of the average 1 OZ!!! Spectacular prices, extremely clean, cozy, and a great lunch menu. It is divided into 2 sections. Half as a restaurant with quiet dining and the other half sells alcohol; multi-functioning as a liquor store and provides the take-out orders. I believe they sell all the bottles they serve in house. EVERYTHING IN THIS RESTAURANT IS HOMEMADE. We came here with no expectations but they really blew any possible judgements away. Will continue to recommend and come back. Perfect view and location right on Ventura blvd in Sherman oaks, close to studio City.<//text>

Very warm and familial service with real Italian chefs. The lady behind the counter on Friday and Saturday is a wonderful historian and mixologist, changing out the specialty cocktails every week-I mean they have chartreuse!

Negroni and Aperol spritz were very well balanced with her homemade, organic bitters.

I had the pappardelle pasta which was very good and the magherita pizza was hearty. I might recommend less cheese and more basil. Tiramisu was exceptional, so well balanced with the coffee fallacies and fluffy vanilla exterior</review>

<Review>I had a mixed experience with this car rental service, so I would recommend using caution if you have to use them. We were having our car repaired just down the street at CBS auto (I posted a separate review for them) and Hertz was within walking distance of the repair shop, so we rented a car from them. I had to return the car a few days later, because the brake pads were worn out. I obtained a second vehicle without any problem with their apologies. I took out the company insurance on the vehicle and was glad I did, because I experienced a hit and run. Thankfully, I had my own photos of what the vehicle looked like prior to my driving it for the first time as there was prior damage not incurred by me. After returning the vehicle, I paid remaining fees with my bank card and then realized a month later they had charged my credit card the exact same fees. They got paid twice! To be fair, I never called them to have it corrected, because at the time I was dealing with a life and death situation and was at the hospital with a family member. I recommend using only one method of payment and staying aware of exactly what you are being charged in case of mistakes. Ask questions every step!

< text>
Our first dining experience at Malibu Farm Restaurant was absolutely wonderful; it did not disappoint. The ambience was spot on, the staff was super attentive and friendly, and the food - app, entree, and dessert - was incredible. Our waiter was knowledgeable about the dishes, and we also chatted with the General Manager, Mitch, who graciously took some time to check in with us. Overall, we loved the chill, positive vibe of the place. Pictured below is the Spaghetti Squash lasagna, which we both ordered, and it was super flavorful. Needless to say, we polished the plates off. And the ice cream, with a dollop of homemade cream at the top, holy cow... definitely save some room for that at the end. All in all, we can't wait to return. Please continue to support Malibu Farm!</text>

< Review>
Everyone is talking about this restaurant in Malibu for their freshness and good food. I have seen a lot of Instagram pictures of this restaurant. Even the social media app from China has voted this restaurant as a hot internet sensation. Many internet influencers have raved about this restaurant too.

The scenery is spectacular with full view  of the beach from the pier. We saw many tourists from out of town who saw this restaurant on Instagram. We got a seat right in front of the beach with a beautiful view.

Unfortunately, with Covid-19, there is no more full table services. You had to order the food first and then find a seat to sit down. The server will bring the food out to you.

For the food, we were a bit disappointed. After reading about all the rave reviews, we had high expectations for the taste and flavors. Unfortunately, the cauliflower crust pizza was not too good. The chicken is so hard to chew and the crust was saggy. It's totally not worth $33 for a 6" pizza. My wife's order was not too good either, the Nachos was stale and the cheese was a bit hard. Maybe it's been waiting on the counter for awhile before it was taken out to us. The price tag of $22 is way over priced for a nacho. I think we should have try their pier Cafe instead.<//Review>

< Text>
Stopped by after a hike to relax and enjoy some of the amazing views! I had a glass of Chardonnay (very heavy pour ) and the oyster shot with lemon, agave, and tequila. It was definitely different from the typical tomato juice based shooters and I recommend giving it a try! We didn't order food but I flipped through the menu and there were a lot of things that looked great. Lots of healthy options and a few vegan/vegetarian options as well!

The night we went it was really chilly so it was easy to get a spot outside but I overheard the server say that it gets super packed when the weather warms up and there's always a long wait for a table.

The outdoor seating is wonderful and they have some spots with couches and comfy chairs. This is perfect for a date night or to bring visiting friends and family.< /Text>

< Review>
The outdoor setting here is beautiful. The menu is full of fresh and delicious options.

The current setup seems rather covid responsible. The tables are arranged to be distant from one another, the stead are all wearing masks, and the cleanliness seems to be on point. They are taking dinner orders from the shielded check in counter as well to keep direct contact with the staff to a minimum.

Overall this restaurant is delicious, and clean, it has great service and a beautiful atmosphere.< /Review>

<Review>I can not say enough of how much I love coming here. The atmosphere won me over initially. Then the chocolate basil ice cream...love at first bite.  Then I came again,  a year later still craving this place and again still delicious. This last time my hubby and I split the spaghetti squash lasagna and the taco trio. I died and went to heaven over that lasagna and I am a lasagna snob in that I think mine is the best.
Coffee here is tasty, but not exceptional.  I am spoiled in that my hubby roasts coffee so I get good fresh coffee most of the time. One thing I do not get though is coffee art and these people know how to make coffee art. I was blown away.  There was a bear in my coffee. Yes, a bear.
They are expensive, but I will come again because I do not live here and it is a treat to come. The wait was not bad, about 5 minutes at 11 am on a Saturday. The heat and lack of shade was a different issue, more canopy would not be wasted. < text>
We were actually going to Nobu ( a few blocks away) but they had nothing available without reservations. So we walked a few blocks to the pier and found this place. When we got there the hosts were a little disorganized and different people were saying the same thing ( there is room for 2 inside, or for 4 outside without shade..). Finally we sat outside in the shade which was nice. We ordered crabs as appetizer (3 pieces very small dish), then 3 salads and a fish taco. The salads were big, tasted fresh and presentation was good. The fish taco was amazing; the fish was fresh and delicious and you could choose to add the potatoes, salad and make it your own way. The atmosphere was nice, casual with families and tourists. And the smoothies! The smoothies were amazing! We ordered 2 peach smoothies and they were better than any Jamba Juice or big smoothie chain store.. I would recommend it to anyone visiting!< /text>

<user_name>Stacy Chang</user_name>< Date>
1551766585859</Date>
< Rating>
5<//Rating>
< Review>
Wasn't a huge fan of the prices, buuuut, it's Malibu and the view is amazing so it shouldn't come at a surprise that this place is pricey.

I came on a Sunday around 10:30AM and there were plenty of seating at their patio (everyone in the group must be here to be seated). The view was stunning and loved the decor of their outdoor seating. It was a tad bit chilly though (dress appropriately to stay warm as there weren't any heat lamps that I know of).

We ordered a few things ranging from their salsa verde egg-wich, tofu spinach tomato scramble (vegan option), vanilla lattes, oj and a bloody mary. I am very hesitant with vegan food usually because I always fear them to be on the bland side, but I was quite blown away with how tasty their tofu scramble was. The use of the butternut squash gave the whole dish this amazing earthy and aromatic but delicious taste to the dish. The pairing of some baby potatoes (lightly salted) gave it the perfect amount of savoriness. I loved the dish. :) Their oj also tasted very refreshing (they said it's freshly squeezed with organic oranges). Everyone else in the group had a great time with their food and dine-in experience. Would definitely try and come back on a warmer day!< /Review>

< user_name>
Umer Vakil<//user_name>
< Review>
Great place to come for the view, can see the pier and the Malibu coast on the left. It gets pretty chilly amd windy here in late December so keep that in mind if you come.

There is a deck area thats has sofas and a direct view. There are glass wind shields so it makes it slightly wamer than rest of the outdoors sitting area. We originally sat in the non-deck area - the staff was very accomodating when we asked them to move us ahead.

The servers were fast and attentive. I had the Grass-fed beef burger and it was juicy, tender and very filling aside from looking great. The bottom of the bun was crispy and the cheese tasted great. Stayed for coffee later. Just a slight but on the expensive side overall - especially the coffee.

The latte came cold once - we asked for it again and they brought it perfect and removed it off our cheque for the mistake. Great service!<//Review>
